# <a name="obsolete-types-in-the-net-framework"></a><span data-ttu-id="1ba9c-102">.NET Framework'teki eski türler</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="1ba9c-102">Obsolete Types in the .NET Framework</span></span>
<a name="introduction"></a> <span data-ttu-id="1ba9c-103">Bu makaledeki tablolar, artık kullanılmayan türler listesinde [!INCLUDE[net_v45](../../../includes/net-v45-md.md)] ve [!INCLUDE[net_v46](../../../includes/net-v46-md.md)], derleme tarafından düzenlenmiş.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="1ba9c-103">The tables in this article list the types that are obsolete in the [!INCLUDE[net_v45](../../../includes/net-v45-md.md)] and the [!INCLUDE[net_v46](../../../includes/net-v46-md.md)], organized by assembly.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="1ba9c-104">Eski türler ve önerilen alternatifleri her derlemede bir listesini görmek için aşağıdaki bağlantıları kullanın.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="1ba9c-104">Use the following links to see a list of the obsolete types and the recommended alternatives in each assembly.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="1ba9c-105">Bu tür geçersiz olduğundan, tüm üyeleri de artık kullanılmıyor.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="1ba9c-105">Because these types are obsolete, all their members are also obsolete.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="1ba9c-106">.NET Framework Sınıf Kitaplığı'nda ek eski üyeler listesi için bkz. [eski üyeler](obsolete-members.md).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="1ba9c-106">For a list of additional obsolete members in the .NET Framework class library, see [Obsolete Members](obsolete-members.md).</span></span>

 <span data-ttu-id="1ba9c-925">Aşağıdaki bölümlerde, Microsoft derlemelerde eski türleri listelenmektedir.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="1ba9c-925">The following sections list the obsolete types in Microsoft assemblies.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="1ba9c-926">Bu derlemeler, ayrı bir dil (örneğin, Microsoft.JScript.dll'ye veya Microsoft.VisualC.dll) hedef derlemeler gibi özel amaçlı derlemelerdir.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="1ba9c-926">These assemblies are special-purpose assemblies such as assemblies that target an individual language (for example, Microsoft.JScript.dll or Microsoft.VisualC.dll).</span></span>

### <a name="assembly-iehostdll-and-ieexecexe"></a><span data-ttu-id="1ba9c-927">Derleme: IEHost.dll ve IEExec.exe</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="1ba9c-927">Assembly: IEHost.dll and IEExec.exe</span></span>
